 Madan Sabnavis, chief economist at CARE Ratings, asked, "how much more effective is this scheme than the existing schemes?" Will this give more credit to MSME sector? The difference between the new announcement and the existing policies is very minor
 'emsamai package main sarkari inspectoron se utpeeda se aazaadee, panjikrut upakramon ke liye jiesti portal ke jariye lone, lone par zyada byaaj riyaayat (maujuuda 3 fisadi ke bajaae 5 fisadi) or saarvajanik kshetra ke upakramon ke liye kisi mahila dwaara sanchalit emsamai se anivaary kharid (kul kharid kaa 3 fisadi tak) sareekhe kai vaade shaamil hai
 Employing about 12 crore people and about 6
 5 karod kii taadaad vaale emsamai kshetra ke liye ye saare kadam ummid kii kiran ke rup main najar aane chahie the
 Demonetisation in November 2016 and the implementation of GST a few months later, led to a severe shortage of working capital with the sector
 phir jab bhartiya rigerv bank (arabiai) ne duubat karjon ke punarbhugtan ko lekar maanak kade kar die tab to rin milanaa or bhi dubhar ho gaya

 ek ghante se bhi kam samay main 1 karod rupye tak ke karj ko online manjuur kar dene ke vaade ko lekar bhi logon main kaaphi sanshay he

 The book of Yatindra Mishra's writing is quite extensive
 bahuvidh vishyon ke parkhi is lekhak ne apane shodhaparakh lekhan kii dhak keval hindi main hi nahin samooche bhartiya sahitya par chodi he
 His books written or edited include essays on demonstrative stories 'vismay Ka Bakhan', 'kunwar Narayana: Sansar', 'kunwar Narayan: Presence' and 'many Times' on poet Kunwar Narayan, 'beauty of Art' in four volumes
 , The diary compilation 'open sky of directions', 'A word as much as yours is true' and 'bhairavi', a Hindi rewrite of the words of Kannada Shaiv poetess Akk Mahadevi

 ayodhya ke sangithik itihaas par 'ayodhya kii sangeet parampara' tathaa faijabad ke itihaas, samskruti evam samaaj par saanskrithik gajetir ke rup main 'shaharnama' naamak kitaab ke alaava 'agyeyah jitna tumhaara sach he', bhi prakashit ho chuke hai
 English of 'girija' and 'vibhas'; The Urdu and Ayodhya series of poems of 'char Julahe' and 'miles Se Din' have been translated into German
 apane prachur lekhan ke liye yatindra mishra ko tamaam bade puraskaron se nawaja ja chukaa he, jisamen raja foundation puraskaar, uttar pradesh sangeet naatak academy puraskaar, ech ke trivedi smriti yuva patrakarita puraskaar, bharat bhushan agarwal smriti puraskaar, bhartiya bhashaa parishad yuva puraskaar, hemanth smriti kavita sammaan, rajeev gandhi rashtriya ekta puraskaar, parampara ruturaj sammaan sahit bhartiya gyanpith fellowship sahit kai anya puraskaar mil chuke hai

 Excerpts: 1
 sur or sangeet ke sadhak aapke mukhya vishay rahe hai? isaki vajah?yatindra mishrah yah sahi he ki idhar ke varshon main maine sangeet ke saadhakon ke jivan or unki kala ko apane lekhan kaa vishay banaaya he
 This has been done spontaneously
 isliye bhi ki mujhe lagata he ki kalaon or libral arts ke kshetra ke mahatvapurn kalakaaron kii sadhana par vistaar se kaam hona chahie
 That needs to be done not only by writing, but also through audio-video medium
 sangeet saadhakon par likhnaa meraa priy kaam rahaa he
 i am a music lover, i try to understand the nuances of it and try to find taste in it and express it by writing, which in a broad sense causes the taste of common people
 isliye likhakar pathakeey samaaj main sangeet va kalaon ke bare main utsukata jagaane kii koshish bhar karata hoon
 2
 sangeet or sur ke saadhakon ke nijee jivan or unki srijan yatra main aap ko koun zyada aakarshith karata he?yatindra mishrah yah kahana thodaa mushkil he ki nizi jivan zyaada aakarshith karata he yaa ki srijan yatra
 In a way, you will find that both are complementary to each other
 kabhi jivan main se srijan jhaankata he or kabhi srijan ke bahaane ham jivan ke prati us kalakaar kii drushti ko pakad pate hai
 If i talk about the example of my book, i would like to say in the context of 'lata: sur-gatha' that i wrote a book on Lata Mangeshkar ji covering the same part of her life, which is somewhere her musical struggle , Told the story of his grooming process and his flourishing in that art
 jo chizein jivan se sambandhit thim or unka koi bahut gaharaa sambandh sidhe unke sangeet se nahin judata tha, use maine nahin likhaa
 So in this way you can say that if there was an internal relationship between the two, then it would work for both my writer and the reader
 keval vyaktigat zindagi, phir vah kisi kii bhi kyon na ho, samaaj or duniya ke liye har str par jaanane kii baat nahin hai
 Privacy also has dignity, which should be maintained as soon as possible
 pustak ansh- akhtari: soz or saz kaa afasaana; daastaan malikaa-e-ghazal kii3
 You have written books on such personalities as Ustad Bismillah Khan, Girija Devi, Lata Mangeshkar and Sonal Mansingh
 begum akhtar ko inke bich aap kahaan pate hai?yatindra mishrah main khushnaseeb hoon ki mujhe ustad bismilla khaan, lata mangeshkar, girija devi or sonal maansingh jaise bade kalakaaron par kuch kaam karne kaa mauka mila
 i accept from every platform that a greater experience than writing a book on all these has been to go through the creation process which was achieved due to the respect of these idols
 â€˜lata : sur-gaathaâ€™ jaisi pustak bahut padhi or saraahi gayi, yah mere liye behad khushi kii baat he
 
 
 
 magar isse badi baat mere us jivananubhav kii bhi he, jo maine aadarniya lata ji ke saath, saat-aath saalon tak baat karte hue guzaarin or unke nazadik rahakar parshvagayan kii duniya kii rochak kahaniyaan sunin
 Amidst all this, i find the story of Begum Akhtar Sahiba equally interesting, inspiring and meaningful
 unka jis tarah kaa jivan tha or tawaayph parampara se upar uthakar kis tarah vah begum banane kaa qirdaar akhtiyaar karti hai, use jaananaa ek had tak us daur ke saamaajik, rajnatik dhaanche ko bhi samajhnaa he
 Today he is getting more than forty five years, and in these fifty years, his fame has increased
 unako sunne or unki tarah gane vaali ek puri peedi hi maujuud he or lagaataar nayi peedi bhi usamen shaamil ho rahi he
 In such a situation, the task of collecting their memories and handing over their heritage to the new generation seemed to be an important thing
 hindi main durbhaagya se vah ab tak hua bhi nahin tha
 Because of this, i found it relevant to work on Begum Akhtar
 4
 Tell us something about the book 'akhtari: Soz and Saaz Ka Afsana? Yatindra Mishra: This book has been edited by researching the life of Begum Akhtar
 isamen is baat kaa vishesh dhyaan rakhaa gaya ki unki sangithik-yatra or jivan se sambandhit un sari chizon par ek vimarsh taiyaar kiya jaae, jisase akhtaribai faizaabadi se begum akhtar tak ke lambe safar kaa jayja liya ja sake
 In addition to my own articles and comments, articles have been written by experts in music and Begum Akhtar, including Iqbal Rizvi, Dr
 rakhshanda zaleel, kunal re, saleem kidawai, shila dhar, dow
 Scholars such as Praveen Jha and Mamta Kalia are included
 sangeet jagat ke dheron bade fanakaaron ne bhi yahan begum sahiba ke liye kalam chalaayi he
 Among these, one can read the comments of Shruti Sadolikar, Shubha Mudgal, Aneesh Pradhan, Kaumudi Munshi, Malini Awasthi etc
 saath hi unki do pramukh shishyaaon se lambi baatcheet bhi pustak kaa aakarshan he, jinamein shanti hiranand ji or reeta ganguli ke naam liye ja sakate hai
 To a lesser extent, 'akhtari: Soz and Saaz Ka Afsana' is a historical text-like document on the life of Begum Akhtar in the face of Dastangoi, with the story of his becoming malika-e-ghazal
 5
 Writing on Begum Akhtar, what influenced you most of her life? Yatindra Mishra: The aspect of Begum Akhtar Sahiba's life that impressed me the most is her liberated life
 kis tarah pichhali shatabdi ke purvarddh main ek gayika or film abhinetri apni shaksiyat ke belos andaaj, shystagi, udaartaa or kalakaari ke chalate ek bade qirdaar main dhalati he, use padhanaa or samajhnaa us daur ke saanskrithik va raajnneetik sandarbhon ko jaanane kii tarah tha
 In light of all these things, i see Begum Akhtar as a great funkar and equally big human being
 ise pakadaney kii hi koshish maine kii he

 yah kitaab kin logon ke liye upyogi he?yatindra mishrah yah qitaab sirf sangeet-premiyon yaa begum akhtar ke kadradaanon ke liye hi upyogi nahin he
 i think those interested in history and social science will also like 'akhtari'
 ek vishesh daur main hue kisi vishisht charitra ko lekar bune gayi sandarbhon ke tahat likhi gayi qitaaben us daur kaa bhi sansmaran bataati hai

 ' Greece's parliament has supported the government's reform plan with austerity measures to get a third relief package, but the government is also shocked by some mps going against the proposal
 sudhaar yojana sambandhi is prastaav main sarkaar ko adhikrut kiya gaya he ki vah antarrashtriya rindaataaon ke saath saptahanth ke dauraan sulah samjhaute ke aadhaar ke rup main iskaa istemaal kar sakati he
 In favor of the resolution, 251 votes were cast in the 300-member Parliament, while 32 mps voted against it and eight mps as 'present'
 'maujuud' sansadeey niyamon ke tahat ek aisi vyavastha he, jise anupasthiti kii shrenee main rakhaa jaataa he
 Those who voted as 'present' or absent, as well as two members who voted against the proposal, are members of the Syriza Party, the leftist party of Prime Minister Alexi Ciparas
 unki party ke sadasyon ke is prakaar vyavhaar karne se sipraas kii sarkaar kii sthirataa ko lekar hi sawaal paidaa ho gaye hai
 Two ministers who have expressed their displeasure over the proposal include Energy Minister Panajiotis Lafajanis and Social Security Minister Dimitri Sratolis
 iske saath hi party ke ek pramukh sadsy or sansad ke spikar joe konsatantopoulo bhi iske virodh main dikhe
 Lafajanis, in a statement issued to the press, stated his strong and unambiguous objection to the proposal, "I support the government, but i do not support the austerity program of neo-liberal regulation and privatization
" 
 
 kyonki isse mandi, garibi or museebaton kaa dushchakr lambey samay tak chalegaa
 Former Finance Minister Yannis Warofakis, who resigned this week, was absent from voting due to family reasons
 unhone twitor par likhaa ki vah saptahanth kaa samay apni beti ke saath bitaa rahe hai, jo australia se ai he
 However, he sent a letter stating that if he had been present in Parliament, he would have voted in favor of the motion
 lekin is patr ko sansadeey niyamon ke tahat 'haa' vot ke rup main gina nahin ja saktaa tha
 All opposition parties voted in favor of the proposal, except for the Nazi-inspired Golden Dawn and the Communist Party
 sarkaar dwaara pesh kiye gaye prastaavit upayon main karon main vruddhi or pension kharch main katautee karnaa shaamil hai
 This would surely hurt the people of Greece, who had voted overwhelmingly against a similar plan a few days earlier
 tippaniyan But if the new proposal is approved by Greece's international lenders, it will provide long-term financial support to Greece, which has suffered six years of recession

 unhen bhrashtachar or kaale dhan kii samasya kaa koi samaadhaan dena chahie, anyathaa desh unhen bhi jimmedaar tehraayega
 " manmohan singh par sidhaa nishaanaa sadhate hue ramdev ne kaha, "aap apni beijjati kyon kara rahe hai, yadi aap kaala dhan waapas nahin laa sakate to meri tarah baba ban jaaie
 You are from the Sikh community, and many Sikh Gurus have sacrificed for good works
 main aapse anurodh karata hum ki unase kuch sikhie or desh kii seva kiijie
 " ramdev ne nau agast ko ramlila maidan main apana anshan shuru kiya tha
 He said that he is not a loser
 balki vah kaale dhan or bhrashtachar ke khilaaf kai raajnneetik dalon ko ek manch par laane main safal hue hai
 Ramdev said, "had there been a vote on black money in Parliament on Monday, the government would have fallen
 hamen un dalon kaa bhi samarthan mila he, jo sattadhari gathbandhan ko samarthan de rahe he
 " dilli police ne ramdev or upasthit jansamooh se aagrah kiya ki swatantraaa diwas samaaroh se pehle suraksha kaarnon se stadium khaali kar den
 The stadium falls on the route from where the Prime Minister will fly the tricolor to the Red Fort
 ramdev ne samarthakon se stadium chhodane ke liye kaha or kaha, "yadi ham chahen to pradhanmantri ko swatantraaa diwas par tirangaa fahraane se roak sakate hai, lekin yah koi raajnneetik aayojan nahin he
 Millions of freedom fighters have given their lives to us, and we salute it
 " Ramdev further said, "we are not beggars
 ham apane adhikaar maang rahe hai or yadi hamen hamaara adhikaar nahin miltaa to ham iske liye ladenge
 " ramdev ne kaha ki congress sabase bhrasht party he or congress kaa ek bhi sadsy 2014 ke aam chunaav main nirvaachit hone laayak nahin he
 He said, "tell people that the Congress is responsible for making them poor
 congress sabase bhrasht party he or iskaa naam bhrashton kii suchi main sabase upar likhaa janaa chahie
 " gyaat ho ki ramdev or unke samarthakon ko somvaar ko us samay hiraasat main le liya gaya tha, jab ve sansad bhawan ke liye march kar rahe the
 He was then brought to Ambedkar Stadium
 baba ramdev dwaara congress or pradhanmantri par kiye gaye hamalon par congressi netaaon ne bhi tikhi bayaanbaji he
 Congress leaders also accused Baba of using indecent language
 company maamalon ke kendriya mantri em
 Veerappa Moily said, "the way in which he (ramdev) is using indecent language, it shows that he has got the license to speak against those in power
 sanvaidhanik padon kaa sammaan karnaa chahie
 " moili ne kaha, "unhen yah samajhnaa chahie ki sansad kii sthapana desh ke samvidhan se hui he or samvidhan swatantraaa senaniyon ke balidanon se bana he
 He does not understand this language
 vah sansadeey bhashaa bhul gaye

 yah unke liye jaruri he
 "comments soochna or prasaaran mantri ambika soni ne kaha, "mujhe nahin pataa ki koun kya kah rahaa he or kyon kah rahaa he

 " congress pravaktaa manish tiwari ne kaha ki sarkaar pichley kuch varshon se uthaae gaye kadamon ke bare main lagataar bataati aa rahi he
 He said that it would be wrong to say that the government is not taking action
 ramdev ne do bacchon ke haathon nibu pani pikar ambedkar stadium main apana paanch divasiy anshan samaapt kiya
 Addressing a large gathering at the stadium, he said, "I am ending my fast at the stadium, but the movement will continue till our demands are met
" " unhone apane samarthakon se kaha, "aap jab apane gharon ko jaaen to aasapaas ke logon ko congress ke bare main bataaen

 " Delhi Police urged Ramdev and the people present to vacate the stadium for security reasons before Independence Day celebrations
 stadium us maarg par padataa he, jahaan se hokar pradhanmantri laal kile par tirangaa fahraane jaaenge

 " Ramdev and his supporters were taken into custody on Monday while they were marching to Parliament House

 sansad kaa satr 12 agast ko khatm ho jayega, or pradhanmantri narendra modi ne is bill ko apni sarkaar ke agenda main sabase upar rakhaa he
 
 
 Finance Minister Arun Jaitley is expected to meet Congress leaders Ghulam Nabi Azad and Anand Sharma on Thursday to reach an agreement on the bill
 
 
 darasal, jetali kii yah mulaakaat tab tay hui, jab sansadeey kaarymantri anant kumaar ne rajyasabha main congress ke varisht netaaon azaad or sharma tak pahunch banaai
 
 
 Significantly, despite some victories in the recent Rajya Sabha elections, the government is in the minority in the Upper House, and the Congress is still the largest party in the House
 
 
 philhal aisa lagata he ki donon paksh ek-duusare kii baat ko samajhane or shaayad maan lene ke liye bhi taiyaar ho gaye hai
 
 
 With the introduction of GST, many different central and state taxes will be replaced by a single tax across the country, and India will become an 'integrated market' with more than one billion consumers
 
 
 jiesti ko prabhavi banane ke liye laayaa gaya sanvaidhanik sanshodhan prastaav nichle sandan loksabhaa main paarit ho chukaa he, jahaan sarkaar ke paas shandaar bahumat maujuud he, lekin yah rajyasabha main atka hua he, jahaan congress va vamadal jaise anya kuch dal isamen badlaav kii maang kar rahe hai
 
 
 The Congress wants the government to set the maximum rate of GST to 20 percent, and include this rate in the constitution amendment, while the government says that to do so, it will have to amend the constitution every time
 
 
 
 lekin ab congress ne kar kii dar ko jiesti se sambandhit sahaayak dastavezon main darj karwaane par sahamat hone ke sanket die hai
 
 
 Apart from this, the Congress also wants to remove the one percent additional tax proposed by the government, which will have to be given when goods are brought across or taken from the states border
 
 
 is prastaav kaa uddeshy tha ki un rajyon ko bhi muawza mil sake, jo utpaadan par zyaada dhyaan dete hai
 
 
 The third major demand of the Congress is that the Finance Minister should increase the powers of the Council, which will be created to resolve the revenue sharing disputes between the states
 
 
 tippaniyan The government has already stated that it has agreed to these changes suggested by the Congress
 
 
 haalanki trinmul congress, samaajawaadee party, bahujan samaaj party, biju janata dal or janata dal united jaise kshetreey dal is bill ko samarthan dene ke liye sahamat ho chuke hai, or unke samarthan ke baad sarkaar ko aavashyak do-tihaai bahumat paa lenaa sambhawatah mushkil nahin hoga, lekin unhen congress kaa samarthan isliye zaruri he, taaki vah sansad kaa kaarywahi ko chalane de, or bill pesh kiya ja sake
 
 
 Sources say that anyway the government wishes to keep this important bill as a unanimous proposal
 
 
 bill ko lekar kisi samjhaute par pahunchane ke uddeshy se guuruuvaar ko vittamantri arun jetali ke congress netaaon gulam nabi azaad or anand sharma se mulaakaat karne kii sambhaavna he
 
 
 Actually, Jaitley's meeting was decided when Parliamentary Affairs Minister Ananth Kumar reached out to senior Congress leaders Azad and Sharma in Rajya Sabha
 
 
 gauratlab he ki haalia rajyasabha chunaavon main kuch jeet milane ke baavjood sarkaar ucch sadan main alpamat main he, or congress ab bhi sadan main sabase bada dal he
 
 
 For now, it seems that both sides have agreed to understand and perhaps agree on each other
 
 
 jiesti ke aane se dheron alag-alag kendriya or raji karon ke sthaan par deshbhar main ek hi kar lagu ho jayega, or bharat ek arab se bhi zyaada upabhoktaaon vaala 'ekikrut bazaar' ban jayega
 
 
 The constitutional amendment proposal to make GST effective has been passed in the lower Parliament Lok Sabha, where the government has a great majority, but it is stuck in the Rajya Sabha, where some other parties like Congress and Left parties are demanding changes in it
 Have been
 
 
 congress chaahati he ki sarkaar jiesti kii dar kii adhiktam seemaa 20 pratishat tay kar de, or is dar ko samvidhan sanshodhan main shaamil kar de, jabaki sarkaar kaa kahana he ki aisa karne par daron main badlaav karne ke liye har baar samvidhan main sanshodhan karnaa padegaa
 
 
 But now Congress has indicated to agree to file the tax rate in the supporting documents related to GST
 
 
 congress iske alaava sarkaar dwaara prastaavit ek pratishat atirikt kar ko bhi hatwanaa chaahati he, jo vastuon ko rajyon kii seemaa se aar-paar laane yaa le jane par dena hoga
 
 
 The purpose of this proposal was to provide compensation to those states which pay more attention to production
 
 
 congress kii teesri badi maang he ki vittamantri us parishad ke adhikaron ko badha den, jo rajyon ke bich rajasav bantwaare ke vivaadon ko sulajhane ke liye banaai jaaegi
 
 
 The comments sarkaar pehle hi congress dwaara sujhaaye gaye in badlaavon par sahamat ho jane ke bare main bataa chuki he
 
 
 Although regional parties like the Trinamool Congress, Samajwadi Party, Bahujan Samaj Party, Biju Janata Dal and Janata Dal United have agreed to support the bill, and after their support, the government may not find it difficult to get the required two-thirds majority
 They will, but they need the support of the Congress, so that it can allow the Parliament to proceed, and the bill can be introduced
 
 
 sutron kaa kahana he ki vaise bhi sarkaar kii ichha is mahatvapurn bill ko sarvasammati se laae gaye prastaav ke rup main rakhane kii he
 
 
 For now, it seems that both sides have agreed to understand and perhaps agree on each other
 
 
 jiesti ke aane se dheron alag-alag kendriya or raji karon ke sthaan par deshbhar main ek hi kar lagu ho jayega, or bharat ek arab se bhi zyaada upabhoktaaon vaala 'ekikrut bazaar' ban jayega
 
 
 The constitutional amendment proposal to make GST effective has been passed in the lower Parliament Lok Sabha, where the government has a great majority, but it is stuck in the Rajya Sabha, where some other parties like Congress and Left parties are demanding changes in it
 Have been
 
 
 congress chaahati he ki sarkaar jiesti kii dar kii adhiktam seemaa 20 pratishat tay kar de, or is dar ko samvidhan sanshodhan main shaamil kar de, jabaki sarkaar kaa kahana he ki aisa karne par daron main badlaav karne ke liye har baar samvidhan main sanshodhan karnaa padegaa
 
 
 But now Congress has indicated to agree to file the tax rate in the supporting documents related to GST
 
 
 congress iske alaava sarkaar dwaara prastaavit ek pratishat atirikt kar ko bhi hatwanaa chaahati he, jo vastuon ko rajyon kii seemaa se aar-paar laane yaa le jane par dena hoga
 
 
 The purpose of this proposal was to provide compensation to those states which pay more attention to production
 
 
 congress kii teesri badi maang he ki vittamantri us parishad ke adhikaron ko badha den, jo rajyon ke bich rajasav bantwaare ke vivaadon ko sulajhane ke liye banaai jaaegi
 
 
 The comments sarkaar pehle hi congress dwaara sujhaaye gaye in badlaavon par sahamat ho jane ke bare main bataa chuki he
 
 
 Although regional parties like the Trinamool Congress, Samajwadi Party, Bahujan Samaj Party, Biju Janata Dal and Janata Dal United have agreed to support the bill, and after their support, the government may not find it difficult to get the required two-thirds majority
 They will, but they need the support of the Congress, so that it can allow the Parliament to proceed, and the bill can be introduced
 
 
 sutron kaa kahana he ki vaise bhi sarkaar kii ichha is mahatvapurn bill ko sarvasammati se laae gaye prastaav ke rup main rakhane kii he
 
 
 With the introduction of GST, many different central and state taxes will be replaced by a single tax across the country, and India will become an 'integrated market' with more than one billion consumers
 
 
 jiesti ko prabhavi banane ke liye laayaa gaya sanvaidhanik sanshodhan prastaav nichle sandan loksabhaa main paarit ho chukaa he, jahaan sarkaar ke paas shandaar bahumat maujuud he, lekin yah rajyasabha main atka hua he, jahaan congress va vamadal jaise anya kuch dal isamen badlaav kii maang kar rahe hai
 
 
 The Congress wants the government to set the maximum rate of GST to 20 percent, and include this rate in the constitution amendment, while the government says that to do so, it will have to amend the constitution every time
 
 
 
 lekin ab congress ne kar kii dar ko jiesti se sambandhit sahaayak dastavezon main darj karwaane par sahamat hone ke sanket die hai
 
 
 Apart from this, the Congress also wants to remove the one percent additional tax proposed by the government, which will have to be given when goods are brought across or taken from the states border
 
 
 is prastaav kaa uddeshy tha ki un rajyon ko bhi muawza mil sake, jo utpaadan par zyaada dhyaan dete hai
 
 
 The third major demand of the Congress is that the Finance Minister should increase the powers of the Council, which will be created to resolve the revenue sharing disputes between the states
 
 
 tippaniyan The government has already stated that it has agreed to these changes suggested by the Congress
 
 
 haalanki trinmul congress, samaajawaadee party, bahujan samaaj party, biju janata dal or janata dal united jaise kshetreey dal is bill ko samarthan dene ke liye sahamat ho chuke hai, or unke samarthan ke baad sarkaar ko aavashyak do-tihaai bahumat paa lenaa sambhawatah mushkil nahin hoga, lekin unhen congress kaa samarthan isliye zaruri he, taaki vah sansad kaa kaarywahi ko chalane de, or bill pesh kiya ja sake
 
 
 Sources say that anyway the government wishes to keep this important bill as a unanimous proposal
